mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">追魂（刘进兴）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卓嘎（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">子肃、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">字会梅、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邹昌英、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">左洪涛、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赞查（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赞查（藏）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">达日（藏）都是四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，二人皆因“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿案”而被阿坝县警方拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名分别重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">泽让旦真（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生年月不详，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州人，又叫“洛桑丹增”，阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因帮助同寺僧人彭措（又叫平措，已于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日自焚死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁）以自焚方式（指一种藏人抗议暴政、伸张正义的方式，即藏人自焚者把自己整个奉献出来，以清晰的理智、自愿的心态和惨烈的方式向暴政表达最强烈抗议的无奈选择，以期使公众舆论对极权和高压统治者予以最强烈的谴责或改变对手的情感），纪念中共当局镇压拉萨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>•<span lang="EN-US">14</span>事件三周年，并在阿坝县城洽唐中街实施自焚行动；由于当地僧人和藏人为此举行了大规模情愿示威活动，随与中共军警发生冲突；其随后即被拉萨市警方抓捕、刑拘，并被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康县警方以涉嫌“购买汽油策划，鼓动、帮助自焚罪”执行逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案在四川省马尔康县法院开庭受审，最终被该法院更换罪名，以“故意杀人罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾兵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾兵、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辛国慧、赖平三人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">成都双流区失地农民，维权人士。三人于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年进京上访被抓，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，辛国慧、赖平，曾兵三人涉嫌“寻衅滋事”案在成都西航港法庭开庭审理，未判决。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾春智：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">45</span>岁。湖北省应城市维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，湖北省应城市维权人士曾春智女士因抗议封城期间物业给居民生活物资配送价格过高而组织居民维权，后遭当局报复，当地警方于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日竟然对曾春智女士行政拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日当地警方将其刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被应城市检察院批准逮捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾浩：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东技术师范学院教师、法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年上大学时开始修炼法轮功。曾浩大学毕业后在广州供销学校任教。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功以来，被开除公职，并两次被非法拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年被迫流离失所近两年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年仅因为在<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>空间说说中上传和转载了几个与法轮功内容相关的图片，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日在自家楼下买早餐时被广州市海珠区国保大队、江南中街派出所、青葵居委会强行带走并抄家，被非法关押到广州市海珠区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，广州市海珠区法院非法对曾浩进行开庭，律师指出：本案没有受害人，所有指控的证据都是非法的，曾浩无罪。曾浩现任广东技术师范学院天河学院教师，学校盼他早日回校上课。曾浩是家中独子，父母<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁高龄，幼子才<span lang="EN-US">4</span>岁，都需要他照顾。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">扎西达杰（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1984</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县人，炉霍寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。因中共当局在西藏及其周边各省涉藏地区强硬推行“爱国和法制宣传教育”活动，引发多地藏民强烈不满，四川省甘孜州炉霍县藏民随于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日（即当年中国农历新年初一）举行大规模和平示威活动；该活动随即遭到中共警方严厉的武力镇压和任意抓捕，致使多人被打死打伤及上百人被抓；至<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，已有<span lang="EN-US">36</span>人被中共当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月直至无期徒刑不等的刑期，另有数人被捕后完全失踪；扎西达杰亦因积极参与和平示威游行，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被警方以“参与和带头示威活动”为由从当地炉霍寺抓走刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县法院以“炉火示威活动的主要带头人”判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。此前被羁押于四川省甘孜藏族自治州康定县监狱；目前在何监狱服刑，情况不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">扎西顿珠（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州若尔盖县唐克镇人。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因独自在四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州若尔盖县城，身披佛教旗帜、手举大幅达赖喇嘛画像，以小跑方式在主要大道上开展抗议中共暴政的示威活动，随被当地警方在极短时间内控制、拘捕；据悉，此前其所在村镇藏民多年来一直因土地遭政府强占、暴力逼迁且得不到任何安置，而多次展开过和平请愿活动（含派代表进省城上访、集体静坐、呈交联署信、集会讨公道等），要求政府当局核实土地征用过程是否非法，并予以公正处理，但却无果而终；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，其被阿坝藏族羌族自治州地方当局正式逮捕，并被判处有期徒刑，罪名、刑期不详，服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">扎西杰（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州若尔盖县人。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因拍录阿坝藏族羌族自治州藏人扎西顿珠身披佛教旗帜、手举大幅达赖喇嘛画像，在若尔盖县城大街上进行抗议中共暴政的抗议过程，并传于网上，随被当地警方于<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日左右抓捕、刑拘，具体罪由不详；据悉，此前其所在乡镇藏民长期因土地问题而被政府强占、暴力逼迁，得不到安置等所困扰，村民多次展开和平请愿活动而无果；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，其与扎西顿珠一起被阿坝藏族羌族自治州地方当局正式逮捕，并被判处有期徒刑，罪名、刑期不详，服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">扎西曲英（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，四川省甘孜州道孚县葛卡乡约呷村人，道孚县尼措寺（全名“尼措图桑达杰林寺”，汉文称“灵雀寺”）僧人，印度西藏甘丹寺强孜经学院最高等级“格西拉然巴”经学博士班一年级学生，藏族政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年前往印度，同年进入印度南部西藏甘丹寺强孜经学院学习。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月下旬持中国驻新德里大使馆发放的旅行证返家探亲过程中，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日突然被中共当局毫无理由地强行拘捕，至此失联。后获悉其被当局指控，因在印度期间曾将道孚县境内发生自焚事件的消息披露给媒体，随被视为泄密。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底，经一位藏族政治犯从监狱获释后向其家人传信，家人方才获知，他和扎西曲英在同一个监狱服刑，扎西曲英被监禁在甘孜州首府康定县新都桥镇的四川省甘孜监狱。后经证实，他于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被四川省甘孜州法院以不知名罪名（疑似“泄露国家机密罪等”）重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">扎西文色（也译：扎西旺楚）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年出生，青海省玉树藏族自治州玉树市人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Tashi Wangchuk</span>，藏族企业家，藏语言教育倡导者、维权者。十多年来，扎西文色曾先后有两次被当局拘留经历；早年间，曾因<span lang="EN-US">“</span>非法前往印度<span lang="EN-US">”</span>而被拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，又因在网上发表抗议政府非法占地的言论而遭拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，因青海、甘肃等省的藏区公立中学已停止使用藏语授课，仅将其作为一门母语课程，甚至有些学校完全不授藏语课，引起藏人不满，与此同时，其所在青海省玉树市结古街道办事处亦开始明令禁止当地寺院及私立学校向僧侣以外的民众传授藏语，于是其便在微博上公开发表了对藏语教育逐步被丧失的担忧，此举很快引起当局不满与警觉。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">—9</span>月，为敦促各级政府自觉兑现、维护藏语言合法使用及地位的承诺，其开始上访北京，向中央递交检举信函，揭露藏区地方政府并未支持藏人语言教育的事实，并接受纽约时报记者采访，制作了一个为时<span lang="EN-US">9</span>分钟的视频短片，此举进一步遭致地方政府仇视与嫉恨。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，因其在微博群里再次呼吁，建议青海省人大会议应该敦促地方政府提升双语教育，并雇用更多的会说双语的地方官员，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日即被玉树市警方以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">“</span>危害国家安全<span lang="EN-US">”</span>刑拘，后被玉树市检察院以<span lang="EN-US">“</span>煽动分裂国家罪<span lang="EN-US">”</span>正式批捕，并被移交到地方法院。一直被羁押于青海省玉树州看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，扎西文色涉嫌煽动分裂国家案宣判，青海玉树州中级法院判处扎西文色<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">翟国兴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日早晨在天津河东区万新村菜市场讲法轮功，被警察抓捕到东新派出所。当天中午抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月翟国兴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月关押到天津女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">翟永池：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省绥中县人，法轮功学员。因信仰、宣传法轮功遭多次打压逼迫。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被辽宁省绥中县警方以涉邪教罪刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被转正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日其案在辽宁省绥中县法院开庭受审，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”一审判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。其不服，已上诉到葫芦岛市中级法院，律师递交了开庭申请，即将面临二审。目前被羁押于绥中县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">展振振：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">“佳士事件”被捕人士，北大在校生。系“佳士工人声援团”成员，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7-8</span>月间前去深圳坪山的佳士公司工人维权现场声援。因“佳士事件”被带走调查，有消息指，校方将会对展振振作退学处理，并将展移交警方处理。遭强迫失踪至今。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">詹传云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省长丰县女访民。其家房屋被拆迁、土地被征收，因未获合理补偿而上访。詹传云女士是于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被警方从家中抓捕后刑拘羁押于合肥女子看守所的，被羁押<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天才开庭审理。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，詹传云被敲诈勒索（政府）罪案件在长丰县人民法院第二法庭开庭审理，詹传云女士的律师作了无罪辩护，合肥市<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多位访民到庭旁听案件审理。据悉，案件审理时，公诉人提出的证据被律师驳回，女访民岂能敲诈政府？尤其是敲诈国家暴力机器公安部门，案件审理将结束时，迫于证据难以支持敲诈勒索罪的法官问被告人詹传云，撤掉敲诈勒索罪变更为寻衅滋事罪行不行？被告人詹传云女士非常坚定的回答，她没有罪。最后陈述时，詹传云女士称自己为自己家房屋被拆迁和土地征收上访维权，她没有罪。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">战玉彩：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年三十二岁的女研究生、济南法轮功学员。在中共对法轮功持续至今近二十年的迫害中，战玉彩女士第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被判刑。她在<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被济南历下区法院判刑四年；随后她丈夫杜泽洲被济南长清区警察跟踪抓捕，被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，至今仍在山东省监狱关押迫害。战玉彩女士<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚九点左右，从济南历下区姚家庄去往政法学院的路上张贴真相不干胶时，当场被后面跟踪的济南历下区智远派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，战玉彩被抓捕到济南市看守所非法关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被济南市历下区法院开庭，被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张宝成：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1959</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日出生，北京市人，自由职业者，资深民主人士，新公民运动参与者，北京西单广场举牌十公民之一。六四<span lang="EN-US">30</span>周年临近，中共当局的维稳镇压措施愈来愈严厉，北京民主维权人士张宝成也被抓捕、抄家。据张宝成妻子刘珏帆介绍：“北京时间<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日零时许，女儿接到张宝成用家里座机打出的电话，他又被抓了，正在抄家，警察说是涉枪。 张宝成不可能涉枪，我怀疑张宝成被抓与他推特转发有关即将来临的敏感日帖子有关。” 因于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年起开始积极参与推动中国的民主活动，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年春被北京市警方关押；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年年底，又因声援刘远东而被警方拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，再次因积极参与“官员财产公示”活动，于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，张宝成与袁冬等人同时被北京市公安局公共交通安全保卫分局以涉嫌“非法集会罪”刑事拘留，并被关押于北京市海淀区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被北京市警方正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被北京市海淀区法院以“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”开庭审理；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被北京市海淀区法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，刑满释放；据悉，因其在狱中曾遭受虐待。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张成武：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东潍坊市昌乐县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午，昌乐县马宋镇张家庄村张成武在家中被警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被山东青州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张春蕾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西忻州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，张春蕾因要求各级政府公开关于迫害法轮功的政策而被非法抓捕。后被批捕，起诉。罪名是利用邪教破坏法律实施罪。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午忻州市忻府区法院开庭审理张春蕾利用邪教破坏法律实施案，文东海律师作为辩护律师参与开庭审理，该案检察院不让辩护律师阅卷，不接收辩护律师手续，不听取辩护律师意见。到了法院仍然不允许阅卷，不公开审理，没有庭审录音录像，在庭上只有法官检察官可以看卷，辩护律师和被告人均不让看卷，辩护律师拒绝就检察官口头念的证据目录发表质证意见，申请回避驳回，要求复议法官认为没有复议权利。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张翠琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽宿州市泗县瓦坊乡维权人士，因被人打伤致残后，不服宿州市泗县法院判决而开始上访讨说法，至今无果。多年来一直向各级政府部门求助，却遭到地方村干部的打压报复，多次被拘禁、拘留、殴打。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日张翠琴被泗县公安局以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，羁押于宿州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张大娥<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张大娥、王龙飞母子是河南省许昌市襄城县茨沟乡五里堡村疫苗受害者家长，系母子。张大娥、王龙飞母子先后被襄城县公安局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑拘、于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日同一天逮捕。王龙飞的父亲王振堂表示，王龙飞被刑拘是因为<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日我们一家人在省政府大门外路边挂维权牌子，求见省长反映我孙子王诺一被疫苗致残的事。王龙飞推着孩子站在路边并没做什么，当时几个特勤人员过来把我拉到一边照我脸上就扇，又把我抬起来扔掉。七十岁的姨奶奶吓得晕倒在地，无奈家人只好把我俩人送进医院做了简单处理。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日一群警察闯进我家，不由分说把我儿子王龙飞带走关押在襄城县看守所，并带走了家里两个手机和亲戚家的一台电脑。当时王龙飞的母亲张大娥不在家，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又把张大娥三个帮忙维权的姐姐带走拘留了五天。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，张大娥在厦门被带回来关押在拘留所，后又被送到许昌看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日乡派出所送来逮捕证，张大娥、王龙飞以寻衅滋事罪被逮捕了。事情要追溯到<span lang="EN-US"> 2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，当时家人带着只有六个月的王诺一，在襄城县防疫站接种乙肝、百白破、口服脊灰糖丸三种疫苗，接种疫苗当晚，孩子哭闹不止，过后几天总是烦躁不安，精神不振，后来开始发烧抽搐。经襄城县人民医院、郑州儿童医院、北京医院等多个大医院治疗确诊为婴儿癫痫痉挛症，脑损伤综合征，精神运动生长迟缓，巨细胞病毒感染。而襄城县疾控中心却诊断为偶合症。他们一家不相信疾控中心的诊断结果，找防疫站协商解决此事反被拘留。此后一家人开始进京上访，襄城县疾控中心领导联合茨沟乡派出所对他家人一次次进行打压拘留，奶奶张大娥曾因上访被多次拘留，孩子爸爸、妈妈、姑姑都被拘留过。这两年多以来，他们为了维权用尽了各种方法，岂料问题没有得到解决，却被冠以“寻衅滋事罪”逮捕。遭遇这么多的打击，一家人泪都哭干了，为给孩子治病已经倾家荡产，奶奶张大娥为孩子治病倾尽一切心血。张大娥母子被刑拘后，众多疫苗受害者家长自发捐款，为王诺一治病。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张迪</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵文静、黄金桔、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张冬宁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">现年<span lang="EN-US">22</span>岁，漫画家，安徽淮南人。曾赴日本。创作过“猪头人身系列”漫画，被中共当局指为“精日”、“辱华”。于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被刑事拘留，现已被批准逮捕。此案消息一出，舆论哗然。因画漫画就遭刑拘逮捕，当下中国大陆因言获罪的程度已经到了令人恐怖的地步。此案在网路上引起强烈关注，已有大陆律师愿意为其免费做无罪辩护。而谴责当局因言治罪的声浪在微信里此起彼伏。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张桂芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨市通河县法轮功学员，哈尔滨医科大学本科毕业，本是通河县妇幼保健院主治医师，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日早，公安局一张桂芝和另一位法轮功学员被绑架。后张桂芝被判刑五年，在黑龙江省女子监狱遭受迫害，曾经被关小号，戴脚镣。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，张桂芝在通河县邮政局邮寄劝善信，邮局工作人员拒邮后，说要请示一下领导。接着“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”国保大队五人，抓捕了张桂芝。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，哈尔滨市依兰县第三法院对张桂芝庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获知，张桂芝被哈尔滨市依兰县第三法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张国兵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东河源维权人士。张国兵有两个孩子的，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日以学生家长身份依法申请公布学校食品安全监督信息。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>时被东源县公安带走，约三小时后被广东河源市公安局人员抄家。搜走手机、身份证、护照、银行卡等物（张没有电脑）。家属两次都问公安人员，是什么事抓人？均回答，不知道，查清楚再说。后获悉<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪名被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张海涛</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年出生，河南省南阳市镇平县籍人，原<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代国企下岗工人，新疆区域电信产品销售者、自由职业者，民主人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被新疆维吾尔族自治区乌鲁木齐市中亚南路派出所警方以涉嫌“煽动民族仇恨、民族歧视罪”抄家、刑事拘留、逮捕；之后被以“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕，羁押于新疆乌鲁木齐市看守所。据悉，其家中银行卡全部被警方冻结，妻子即将生育，生活面临极大困境。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日再次被变更罪名以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”继续超期关押，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被乌鲁木齐中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家罪”、“为境外刺探、非法提供情报罪”重判徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处没收个人财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">12</span>万；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日经新疆乌鲁木齐高级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判。目前在新疆维吾尔族自治区沙雅监狱九监区服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南洛阳市宜阳县寻村镇的张红，因<span lang="EN-US">21</span>年前女儿受到性侵后考虑名誉而接受私了，想不到引起一连串家破人亡加坐牢的悲惨结局！<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年年全国“两会”前，张红在家中又被宜阳县公安局以“寻衅滋事罪”带走，目前已被宜阳县检察院批准逮捕，再次面临牢狱之灾。派出所抓人的理由是：听说张红近期要上访。继而以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，继而再由宜阳县检察院批准逮捕。所谓张红“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”，是张红以上访为由敲诈勒索了政府<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元人民币。据张红的儿子张奇峰说，公安局所谓的强拿硬要完全是胡说八道，针对访民的口袋罪，也由原来的敲诈勒索罪，悄悄地改为了寻衅滋事罪。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="background: white; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张红伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南工行断友。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">日上午</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">点左右，在北京西长街</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">15</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">号中国工行银行总部西大门口，有来自内蒙的南行芝、辽宁沈阳的军嫂赵辉、湖南的彭真爱、湖北的毛秋生、河南的张红伟等被工商银行强迫解除劳动关系的“断友”，拦截了工行董事长易会满的车辆，被北京公安以“扰乱单位秩序”为由处以行政拘留五日。张红伟在行政拘留期满被接回地方河南方城县后，再被以“涉嫌敲诈勒索罪”刑拘。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张红艳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">鞠殿红、梁琴、张红艳、字会梅、杨顺祥、张绍彩六人皆为基督徒，云南省临沧市云县基督教传道人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年因在云南省多地<span lang="EN-US">/</span>州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>市传道和发展信徒，随被当局以涉嫌“参与三班仆人派邪教组织”为罪由抓捕，其住处所在地遭查抄，搜走传道宣传品<span lang="EN-US">1831</span>份、传单<span lang="EN-US">2556</span>份，并从电子设备中提取到的电子文件<span lang="EN-US">82816</span>个等。后被云南省临沧市云县检察院宣布正式批捕，并被指控<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人是邪教骨干分子，“到云南省多地州市秘密聚会、传经布道和发展信徒，继续鼓吹、宣扬世界末日论，培养组织骨干，为秘密传教布道聚会创造条件和提供便利，重建‘三班仆人派’组织体系等”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人分别被云南省临沧市云县法院以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月到<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等。其中，鞠殿红因是要犯，被重判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年；梁琴因是要犯被重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。杨顺祥判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">其余张红艳、字会梅、张绍彩<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人，具体刑期不详。但此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人都因不服判决，都已提起上诉。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张华<span lang="EN-US">: </span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东威海荣成市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年六十岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日清晨，张华在她母亲家中被警察团团围住，被抓走。后张华被非法关押在文登看守所。在看守所被非法关押里，张华被迫害的大脑混沌不清，什么也想不起来。而张华的父母均有残疾，她父亲曾经干过生产队长、村会计、大队书记，临老因劳致残，伤了腰和腿，不能行走，却连个残疾证都没办上；她母亲九十度弯腰，也不能直立行走。俩位八十多岁的老人最敢怒不敢言，只能默默承受。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被关押到济南女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张继新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省长春市朝阳区人，女，因<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年儿子受冤入狱维权而开始上访。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，张继新因为去办事路过正在长春视察总理李克强下榻的南湖宾馆，遭当地在现场执勤警察的盘查并抓捕，并于当日构陷“扰乱公共场所秩序”的罪名刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天后被逮捕。张继新现关押在长春市朝阳看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张贾龙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵阳公民、前知名媒体人、原腾讯员工，<span lang="EN-US">80</span>后，曾因为被美国前国务卿克里接见提及刘晓波而遭腾讯开除工作，近年回到家乡贵阳生活，一直比较低调，新婚未久刚生下幼女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日夜晚九点多被辖区派出所和维稳部门从家中带走，随后被以寻衅滋事罪名刑拘，现关押于贵阳南明区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张建兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李希军和张建兰是山东临沂高新区访民，系母女。临沂市公安局高新区技术产业开发区分局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出具的拘留通知书中显示，将张建兰以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，羁押在临沂市看守所。张建兰的亲属表示，张建兰的母亲李希军也被刑拘，和张建兰关押在一个看守所。但警方没给母亲的拘留通知书。其亲属表示，张建兰已经两个多月不上访了，在家照顾孙女，和刚刚生下来才十几天的小孙子，不知道为什么给拘留了。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张建霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北固安县访民。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月张建侠因上访被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘批捕，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日张建侠的律师去廊坊市看守所会见时得知，张建侠在看守所受到虐待，看守所故意治她，不让她买东西，有钱也不让她花，别人都换上夏装了还不让她换，到现在张建侠还都穿着秋衣秋裤。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张君</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：四川省人，在重庆市巴南区工作，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年左右开始信仰、修炼法轮功，但之后很快即遭到当局的严酷打压。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，当他在重庆市巴南区跳石镇给村民讲述法轮功被无辜迫害的真相时，很快就遭到跳石镇派出所警方的抓捕、刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其案在重庆市巴南区法院第一次开庭审理。但由于原告公诉人无法出示有效证据，律师提出不合法律程序，法院庭审被迫中止。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其案被第二次开庭受审，尽管律师为其作了有力的无罪辩护，面对律师的质询和辩护，公诉人承认其实他们没有任何证据可以证明法轮功是“邪教”，也找不到任何法律法规说法轮功是“邪教”，但是在法庭无任何有效证据的情况下，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日其依然已被重庆市巴南区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”非法秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。其不服提已起上诉，目前被羁押在重庆市巴南区看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张菊紅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">48</span>岁，贵州省贵阳市小河经济技术开发区王武村村民，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信法轮功而屡遭当局骚扰和迫害，曾屡遭绑架，送洗脑班，抄家，拘留等。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月曾被绑架到小河戒毒所十天后，又被强行送到洗脑班三个多月，才被释放。同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其家遭查抄，本人又被传唤，至很晚才被放回。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，因在开阳发法轮功资料，所以她再次被开阳派出所警察抓捕，并被送烂泥沟洗脑班（超过<span lang="EN-US">80</span>天）进行迫害，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日又被送到贵阳市第一看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，张菊红被当地检察院正式批捕。超期关押一年半后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其案在贵阳市花溪区法院开庭审理。张菊红的四位亲人参加了旁听。尽管她的律师为她做了无罪判护，她也一直坚持自己炼法轮功无罪，但依然于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被花溪区法院一审枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。其不服，已提起上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张立君：</span></b><span minor-fareast;">黑龙江省双鸭山法轮功学员、双鸭山市石油公司职工、法轮功学员张立君女，<span lang="EN-US">51</span>岁，据因给公检法警察邮寄法轮功宣传信，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span minor-fareast;">张清香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; minor-fareast;">张仁光<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚九点左右，张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波四人因发真相资料，分别被国保和民权派出所绑架。在张仁光家抄走大量耗材。后全送姚家看守所。大连市沙河口区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日庭审法轮功学员张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波，并判张仁光<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、勒索罚款两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张三曼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张尚信：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛阳刘富村维权村民。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，在洛阳洛龙区刘富村村民不知情的情况下，洛阳市洛龙区关林街道办事处与刘富村村民委员会签订了《关林街道办事处刘富村土地流转合同》，约定：位于刘富村的<span lang="EN-US">295.75</span>亩土地承包经营权转流给洛阳市洛龙区关林街道办事处，用于绿化休闲观光。每年土地流转费用标准以每亩<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>斤粮食的价格计算。这引起了村民的极大愤怒。该协议的签订未征求刘富村村民的意见，也未召开村民大会，明显属于暗箱操作，侵害了广大村民的合法权益。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，刘富村众多村民到洛龙区人民政府上访。洛龙区政府戒备森严，上访无果。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，刘富村村民转向洛阳市政府上访，被其工作人员谩骂殴打，还扣押了二名村民。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，洛阳市公安局洛龙分局向刘富村村民张尚信亲属送达了洛龙公（治）拘通字【<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>】<span lang="EN-US">10300</span>号《拘留通知书》，称“根据《中华人民共和国刑事诉讼法》第八十条规定，我局已于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日<span lang="EN-US">4</span>时将涉嫌聚众扰乱公共秩序、交通秩序罪的张尚信刑事拘留，现羁押在孟津看守所。”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张绍彩：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">鞠殿红、梁琴、张红艳、字会梅、杨顺祥、张绍彩六人皆为基督徒，云南省临沧市云县基督教传道人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年因在云南省多地<span lang="EN-US">/</span>州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>市传道和发展信徒，随被当局以涉嫌“参与三班仆人派邪教组织”为罪由抓捕，其住处所在地遭查抄，搜走传道宣传品<span lang="EN-US">1831</span>份、传单<span lang="EN-US">2556</span>份，并从电子设备中提取到的电子文件<span lang="EN-US">82816</span>个等。后被云南省临沧市云县检察院宣布正式批捕，并被指控<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人是邪教骨干分子，“到云南省多地州市秘密聚会、传经布道和发展信徒，继续鼓吹、宣扬世界末日论，培养组织骨干，为秘密传教布道聚会创造条件和提供便利，重建‘三班仆人派’组织体系等”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人分别被云南省临沧市云县法院以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月到<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等。其中，鞠殿红因是要犯，被重判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年；梁琴因是要犯被重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。杨顺祥判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，其余张红艳、字会梅、张绍彩<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人，具体刑期不详。但此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人都因不服判决，都已提起上诉。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张少杰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，河南省南乐县人，前河南省南乐县基督教三自爱国运动委员会主席、基督教协会会长，第九届南乐县政协委员，南乐县基督教会牧师，中国在押良心犯。长期以来，因其身为牧师，经常帮助弱势群体维权解难，尤其是当信徒的合法权益受到侵害时，均想法给予及时的帮助与维权，随在当地备受信徒的喜爱，但这种行为却与政府某些人的利益发生冲突，随遭到当局的强烈不满和忌恨；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被南乐县警方在无任何法律手续的前提下强行从教会带走，其两个胞妹在众人的陪同下前去公安局要人，也被警察强行带走，其余人等亦遭警方堵截和殴打，之后才得知张少杰已被当地警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，又被追加涉嫌“妨害公务罪”予以批捕，但在起诉书中又显示将“妨害公务罪”变更为“诈骗罪”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，终被河南省南乐县法院以“诈骗罪”和“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。此前曾先后被羁押在河南省南乐县看守所和濮阳市看守所；目前在河南省新乡市河南第二监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张素华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省通化市东昌区法轮功学员，女性，<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁。张素华是<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被通化市警察绑架的，在被非法关押一年半后，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，在未通知本人律师的情况下被非法开庭的。家属从接到通知到开庭也才不足三小时。当天下午一点半，对张素华非法庭审，整个过程仅用了十分钟，草草收场。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，吉林省通化市东昌区法院对张素华非法判刑七年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张树德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁，哈尔滨市双城区新兴乡人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。自幼练习和笃信法轮功。哈尔滨工业大学毕业后，曾应聘于大连理工设计院，后外派到盘锦市高新技术产业开发区工作，是个诚实、可信、敬业的好青年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因居住证到期，张树德到所在地的兴隆台区兴盛派出所办理顺延手续时，当身份证录入相关信息时，警察问他有什么信仰，他称其信仰法轮功，随被拒绝办理居住证，并被威胁要对他调查。三天后，其居室遭搜查，本人被传唤做笔录。<span lang="EN-US"> 6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被双手戴着手铐非法送到盘锦市中心医院检查身体，然后就被强行刑拘于盘锦看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，他被盘锦市公安局兴隆台区分局正式逮捕，并将其案移交到兴隆台区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，检察院案将其案卷移交到兴隆台区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其案被盘锦市兴隆台区法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，张树德被该法院一审枉法重判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。其不服上诉。其所在家乡的亲友得知其被冤判后，立刻决定伸出援手征签营救，同乡的父老乡亲们在极短的时间里，亲自填写上自己的名字或按下红手印，呼吁无罪释放张树德回家，目前已有<span lang="EN-US">1744</span>人签名声援。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张顺新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆喀什地区泽普县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁，在中共对法轮功持续至今近二十年的迫害中，他因修炼法轮功在<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，但他挺过来了。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚十点左右，张顺新被塔西南石油基地公安局（隶属于泽普县公安局）警察冯海洋骗到派出所后，再次被绑架关押抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，新疆喀什地区公安局警察到法轮功学员张顺新家通知亲属，张顺新现被关在农三师图木舒克市盖米里克监狱。亲属这才知道张顺新于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并在亲属、律师不在场的情况下秘密宣判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">澳门居民。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，珠海王家婚礼教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛（澳门居民）被捕。数个月后，珠海市香洲区检察院以“诈骗罪”起诉。控方指魏小妹、李炳新及张涛涉嫌诈骗信徒奉献款，购买房产，构成诈骗罪。据知情人士披露，当局的指控缺乏有力证据，难以成立。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，香洲区民族宗教事务局取缔该教会，并扣留该教会近五十台电脑<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，当局出动数十名公安，拘捕该教会十多名信徒，经过连续审讯及威胁，信徒被迫写下不利于教会领袖的证词。警方最终以诈骗罪刑事拘留该教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛。据知情人士披露，该案由珠海市政法委督办。当局先以“邪教罪”调查此案，但因查无实据，又改为“诈骗罪”问罪，这明显是一起宗教案件。目前，广东珠海王家婚礼教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛（澳门居民）三人，被珠海市香洲区检察院以“诈骗罪”起诉至法院，指当事人诈骗奉献款，上述三人面临判刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张廷福：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁老人张廷福在达州下火车，被达州车站派出所拦截扣押后刑事拘留，问其原因，是重庆上清寺派出所将张廷福上传为网上追逃人员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日重庆维权人士张廷福，被重庆市公安局渝中区分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑拘，现羁押在渝中区看守所。家属经多方投诉后，才于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日拿到刑事拘留通知书，张廷福也从达州转至重庆渝中区看守所，得知成为逃犯的原因，是派出所以其涉嫌寻衅滋事罪，上传为网上追逃。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张为卿：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">29</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁，湖北省咸宁市人，咸宁市咸安区政府宿舍区居民，法轮功学员。因信仰和宣传法轮功备受当局打压迫害，经常被骚扰、跟踪监控。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被咸宁市通城县警方抓捕。开始被关关押在湖北省法制教育所板桥洗脑班，后又被转押至咸宁市看守所，至今未被释放。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张文斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原籍山东、原定今年大学毕业。因<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在微信实名公开发布“习近平下课”、“共产党下课”视频后，其微信被封杀，后又遭强迫失踪，目前处于失联状态。此前他曾因言获罪被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天。张文斌说，自己挺身而出，武汉肺炎疫情是导火索。而这段矛头指向习近平的视频使他又遭遇了强迫失踪。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张五洲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">人权捍卫者、湖北籍、家住广东清远市。张五洲是被关进广州白云区看守所死亡的张六毛的姐姐。张五洲为了给弟弟的不明死亡讨回公道受到打压，开始关注公益和参与一些民主、人权活动。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，广州女律师孙世华在广州荔湾区华林派出所办案时，受到该所民警殴打并遭脱衣检查侮辱。随行的张五洲和梁颂基作为目击者，在网上公开为孙世华作证。广州警方为此报复，以“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕了张五洲和梁颂基。后梁颂基被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半和张五洲<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。张五洲女士于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日当天，前往广州著名风景区白云山，在山上栏杆上打出横幅，上书“勿忘六世，撤回恶法”、“女律师被殴目击证人”等字样，以此纪念<span lang="EN-US">31</span>年前的六四事件，以及反对中共两会刚刚通过的香港国安法的实施。张五洲把该活动拍照及视频发微信朋友圈和其它平台发布后，翌日（<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日）下午<span lang="EN-US">14</span>时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分，广东清远市公安局清城区分局石角派出所以张五洲“涉嫌扰乱公共秩序”为由将其清远市家中传唤带走，随后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日来警方又来抄家。狱中遭受酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁左右，大连市中山区人，原中山区青云小学教师，法轮功学员，良心犯。因信仰法轮功并起诉江泽民，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，被送洗脑班<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在学校上班时间又被大连市国保与民主广场派出所警方联合绑架抓走，家被查抄，电脑及相关法轮功资料等均被搜走。其丈夫孙俊区派出所问询，已被扣押，后得知夫妇二人均被关押在大连市姚家看守所羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其被大连中山区检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年被大连市中山区法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月。其不服提起上诉，大连市中级法院未经二审即对她维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，张霞被送往辽宁省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张小梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏镇江人，维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，张小梅涉嫌“寻衅滋事”案在江苏镇江市润州区法院开庭审理，未宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张小平：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，洛阳公民张小平疑因举报厅级干部被刑事拘留，其丈夫张智斌行政拘留。原因疑是他们向中央巡视组举报原洛阳市市长郭洪昌、李柳身（正厅级干部）。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张小平被洛阳公安局南昌路分局（电话<span lang="EN-US">0379-64316110</span>）抓捕；涉嫌罪名是“寻衅滋事”，<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日早被刑事拘留，现羁押在洛阳看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>号，洛阳政府为了修建西环路，在程序不合法的情况下，对张小平家宅基地上的房屋进行了强拆，张小平也因此被逼自学法律，走上了依法维权抗争之路。张小平通过信息公开、行政诉讼等法律途径获取了一些关于修建道路的政府信息，通过对这些信息的分析，发现了前洛阳市市长郭洪昌、李柳身违法修建西环路造成至少<span lang="EN-US">1</span>亿元国有资产流失的事实。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，张小平就这一事实，实名向驻河南中央第一巡视组<span lang="EN-US">65</span>号邮寄了一封《举报信》，此信查询单显示<span lang="EN-US">3.28</span>日已经妥投。巡视组不但没有保护张小平举报人的身份，此举更是将张小平暴露在被举报人的眼皮之下，被打击报复也是迟早之事； <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">因为举报的事情，张小平接到过威胁电话。关于泄漏举报人信息的问题，张小平通过新浪微博发声质疑，并要求相关部门查处。其最后一个博文发于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，结果，违法人员没得到查处，举报人却被抓了进去。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张绪民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，山东泰安肥城市法轮功学员、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十四岁，原肥城市国土资源局副局长。因坚持修炼法轮功被非法劳教两年、冤判四年六个月。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被肥城市公安局拘留，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被批捕。张绪民被关押在肥城市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，山东泰安肥城市法院判张绪民被<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款三万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张雪春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">微信名海燕，维权人士。于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被沈阳市和平分局以（聚众犹乱社会秩序）罪刑拘，目前关押在沈阳市第一看守所，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日批捕。张雪春家人委托的代理律师向大家征集在北京最高检察院、最高人民法院的目击证人，证明张雪春在按照我国相关法律法规，依法有序向最高人民检察院，最高人民法院，提出司法改革建议过程中，没有任何违法行为，更没有任何犯罪行为以事实，然后走正常法律程序，还当事人以清白，请大家自愿报名，为张雪春出庭作证，证明其当事人无罪。已有上百人目击者报名上庭作证。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张艳华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省长春市法轮功学员。张艳华<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月遭长春净月开发区派出所警察绑架，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份遭净月开发区法院非法庭审，被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并遭非法罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张彦平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">958</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，黑龙江省绥化市人，绥化市北林区林业局新生国有林场退休职工，实名举报人，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年起，因其所属林业局正副局长杨清福、杨国庆（兼国有林场场长）合谋贪污，截留国家退耕还林补助资金等问题，一直实名举报，故而屡遭地方当权者强力打压和逼迫；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2010</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾向绥化市北林区检察院提起官员贪腐举报，该检察院虽在同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-7</span>月查出杨国庆确实贪污<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多万（未含退耕还林补贴资金<span lang="EN-US">413</span>万多元），但终因当权者与司法部门枉法勾结，检察院拒绝为其出具处理结果；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因北林区信访局违反《信访条例》规定，为改变其诉求，竟伪造上访信，将其所要的“土地使用权”更改为“土地所有权”，迫使其投诉案因被认定是“无理诉求”而不能进入复议及诉讼阶段，故其只好进京上访，继续维权；然正因此，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其先后曾在北京被警方<span lang="EN-US">8</span>次行政拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，曾因到黑龙江省信访局反应北林区信访局终结不给手续等违法违纪问题，而遭当局陷害被拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，曾因和与其妹到北京协和医院看病而被北林区地方当局（含林业局、检察院、信访局及警方）截住，将其妹腰椎摔成滑脱、腹腔压出血，之后<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被强行遣返，而后长时间拘留，致其身患重病的老父因家中无人照看而不幸冤死家中；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，曾因在北京给国家领导人邮寄投诉信件而遭警方训诫，两日后又被北林区警方拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日、<span lang="EN-US"> 6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，曾再被北林区公安局分别拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾因到北京天安门看升旗，过安检时被查身份证，又一次被送去久敬庄，并被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；此后，尽管其再没到北京上访，然而<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其突然被绥化市北林区警方以“之前有过<span lang="EN-US">8</span>次行政拘留”为由刑拘，并关押在绥化市看守所；后其虽有<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次暂短取保获释，但<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月其案件又被北林区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪” 起诉至绥棱县检察院，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其被黑龙江省绥棱县法院收监逮捕；次日，其案在绥棱县法院开庭审理，被一审以“寻衅滋事罪”枉法判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日；其不服立即上诉，后经绥化市中级法院二审发回地方法院要求重审，但绥棱县法院竟一拖再拖，至今不予重审。目前被羁押于绥棱县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张永宝</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：辽宁省鞍山市人，法轮功信仰者。因信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日晚在高俊的七岭子家中，张永宝、高俊、、二人被辽阳公安局警察跟踪绑架、构陷，后经辽阳县法院三次庭审，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日二人被一审以犯“邪教罪”分别冤判有期徒刑。其中，高俊被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其不服已提起上诉。张永宝被冤判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张郁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省济宁市人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功而被多次遭当地公安机关骚扰和打压。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日当在其母亲家里发放翻墙软件时，被济宁阜桥派出所获悉而抓捕，当日下午其母亲家被查抄，搜走大量法轮功宣传品及翻墙软件等物品。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，张郁被济宁市公安局中区分局刑事拘留，家属前往派出所打听，有关人员将张郁的手表、钥匙、手机、钱包等交给家属，口头告知其已被批捕。现押在济宁市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张元华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川泸州市纳溪区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年四十八岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午，四川泸州市七名法轮功学员高贤英、董国珍、周明英、张元华、刘忠芬、帅先芳、宋平（男）驱车到泸州市合江县五通镇赶场，被派出所警察抓捕，然后带到合江九支镇派出所审问。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被四川泸州市合江县法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，处罚金六千。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张泽英<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">佳士事件”被捕人士，佳士被捕工人李展妻子<b>。</b>被捕是由于一直坚持为丈夫李展发声，以及继续声援佳士工人维权遭到报复抓捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张展</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代出生，陕西省籍人，上海市浦东新区常驻居民，网络异见人士，公民记者、民主公民。硕士学位，毕业后即在上海谋职工作；因不满中共政府的政治现状，长期在网络平台发布批评“一党专政”、腐败滥权等言论，其做派活跃、内容尖锐而颇具针对性，故而曾多次被上海市警方约谈、传唤及威胁；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年以来，因其在微信等网络平台大量转发香港“反送中”抗议视频及文图资料，尤其是每天自己撰文发声，利用行为艺术等为声援香港举牌，随于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被上海警方传唤，自此失联，后知其被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，其父因受警方威胁，故对外拒透其具体信息；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，终获释放；据悉，羁押期间，其曾被两次做强制性“精神病鉴定”。此前被羁押于上海市浦东新区看守所。张展自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日左右去到武汉报导当地疫情，一直在微信、推特、<span lang="EN-US">YouTube </span>等社交媒体平台上直播武汉的现场情况，并尽其所能地帮助受疫情影响的人维权。张展在武汉实地写了大量关于武汉疫情的真实报道。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在武汉遭“强迫失踪”，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被上海市浦东分局刑事拘留，被控罪名是寻衅滋事，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月遭正式逮捕。现羁押在浦东新区看守所。</span><span
