lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张正廷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省丹东市经济合作开发区访民。张正廷今年已经<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁，其在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日凌晨零点<span lang="EN-US">48</span>分，被辽宁省丹东市驻京维稳人员<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余人，闯入其位于北京市大兴区的暂住地，强行截回辽宁丹东。后被丹东市经济合作开发区公安分局刑拘，理由是张正廷涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”。辽宁省丹东市的台属张正廷，其于<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年投资于丹东市振兴区浪头镇的顺达微孔过滤器厂，到<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，张正廷投资的厂房恰好在丹东市城区公路扩建规划内而需要搬迁。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，地方政府在无任何手续的情况下，出动公安、城管以及社会人员几百号人，对张正廷的顺达过滤器厂层层包围，将厂房夷为平地。张正廷的妻子宋玉洁还被殴打致伤。正是在地方申诉无望的情况下，张正廷、宋玉洁夫妻才不得已进京告御状。想不到，这一告就是<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个年头，且每年的敏感时期都要被维稳，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年十八大前夕，丹东市政府提出给张正廷、宋玉洁夫妇俩<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元维稳补偿费，张正廷拒绝后被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。如此政府却诬陷其为敲诈勒索。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张志江：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赤峰市元宝山区五家镇小石头分金桥村居民，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日晚在大水清道上被喀喇沁旗楼子店派出所警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日上午，赤峰元宝山区五家镇村警李文明领着锦山公安局警察闯到张志江家非法抄家，在家里没人的情况下，搜走了大法书。并将张志江非法关押在喀喇沁旗锦山看守所。之后，喀喇沁旗公安局编造材料，将构陷张志江的案卷上报到喀喇沁旗检察院，检察院以张志江炼法轮功、悬挂真相条幅等理由，非法起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，内蒙古赤峰市喀喇沁旗法院开庭非法庭审法轮功学员张志江。张志江为自己做了无罪辩护。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵帮海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川成都法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，成都市法轮功学员赵帮海、李常秋夫妇因宣传法轮功而被抓捕。后均遭枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑，那年他们的独生女儿十六岁。四年来，失去父母照顾的独生女儿多次要求会见冤狱中的父亲，却遭监狱无情的推诿、拒绝。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵晨宇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">昆明市女教师、法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十五岁，原是昆明市第三十中学一级教师，中文系研究生，是一位学生爱戴的好老师。赵晨宇，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初回西双版纳傣族自治州景洪市探望年迈的母亲，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日刚返回到昆明家中，就被跟踪而来的西双版纳景洪市国保大队警察抓捕、抄家。现被关押在西双版纳傣族自治州景洪市看守所。赵晨宇曾于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵春侠</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，辽宁省辽阳市人，基督徒，辽阳市朝光村基督教家庭教会会计。因其教会为基督教家庭教会，且不愿到中共当局指定的“三自”教会敬拜、聚会，遂遭致当局的严打惩罚；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其被辽阳市太子河区警方突然抓捕刑拘，并被指控教会内部使用了基督徒信仰灵修崇拜书籍及相关印刷品，并在教会的便利店销往其他省市，属于非法买卖行为；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被辽宁省辽阳市太子河区法院以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前被羁押于辽阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵鄂川：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵州省贵阳市法轮功学员。赵鄂川<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点至<span lang="EN-US">11</span>点半遭贵阳市南明区法院被庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，南明区法院告知律师，对赵鄂川判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。赵鄂川提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，律师已经把赵鄂川的上诉状递交到贵阳市中级法院。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵广军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">维权老兵。户籍地是辽宁省盘锦市兴隆台区；他的出生地是黑龙江省望奎县；他当兵在锦州四十军<span lang="EN-US">81056</span>部队；他原工作单位是<span lang="EN-US">(</span>北京<span lang="EN-US">)</span>中石油长城钻探；他多年住北京上访；他被维稳的责任单位是兴隆台区。赵广军走上公民维权之路后，因参与公民维权活动、关注侵犯个案，十数次被关黑监狱，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被行政拘留，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>次被刑事拘留，两次被构陷入狱。近一年以来，赵广军多次遭到绑架、软禁，曾经在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月开始的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月中，相继<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次被限制人身自由。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，赵广军在北京被盘锦警方抓走以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，关押在盘锦市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日赵广军被正式批捕，目前家人已经收到逮捕通知书。赵广军此次被抓捕完全是因言获罪。赵广军于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 11</span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 27</span>日 被盘锦市兴隆台区法院判处寻衅滋事罪，获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵桂春</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：内蒙古赤峰元宝山区法轮功学员。于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬被抓捕到女子监狱，在半年中，家人多次去探视，内蒙古女子监狱每次都阻挠亲人会见。赵桂春，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十二岁。十九年来，在中共对法轮功学员的血腥迫害中，她受尽了苦难。赵桂春曾经在内蒙古图牧吉劳教所被非法监禁<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，遭惨无人道的折磨；流离失所<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月和<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月两次被劫持到赤峰喀喇沁旗看守所关押，绝食抗议迫害一个多月后，出现极其危险的症状，保外就医，被迫流离失所。被非法通缉<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，赵桂春被关押到内蒙古女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵桂荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，现住黑龙江省哈尔滨市道外区。丈夫邢世库是哈尔滨印刷二厂职工，因待遇不公于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月从哈尔滨上访到北京，后被关进“精神病医院”。赵桂荣为了解救“被神经”的丈夫开始上访，上访过程中被哈尔滨官员关进黑监狱累计<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多天，造成赵桂荣精神和身体双重受到严重伤害。维权过程中赵桂荣完成从访民到公民的转化，积极参与公民圈活动，关注社会热点问题，围观敏感事件。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，赵桂荣被从北京押回老家后刑事拘留，涉嫌罪名是“聚众扰乱社会秩序”。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日——国际人权日，哈尔滨市道外区检察院将赵桂荣以“寻衅滋事罪”批捕。检察院指控赵桂荣长期参与全国各地声援围观，尤其是庆安事件（徐纯合事件）冲在最前面，严重扰乱社会管理秩序。现关押在哈尔滨市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵国江</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：湖北省襄樊市人，襄樊铁路客运段职工，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信法轮功，早年曾被非法关押拘禁<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次，<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年被冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，赵国江被襄阳市樊城法院秘密非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，随后被送湖北省范家台监狱八监区服刑。出狱后，因他继续坚持信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日又被襄阳樊城区柿铺派出所警方刑拘，家被搜查，被关押在襄阳市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被襄阳市樊城法院再次以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。后被送往襄南监狱，但被拒收，又被送范家台监狱，因体检不合格拒收，现又关押在襄阳市第二看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵海军：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，黑龙江省哈尔滨市人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月因信仰法轮功，并与其妻等人为中共镇压、迫害法轮功到北京和平请愿，被当局抓捕，先被关押于哈尔滨双城市看守所，后又被送到双城区单城敬老院进行强制洗脑教育，期间因屡受虐待酷刑愤而绝食抗议，当局才不得不于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月将其释放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月因前往北京为法轮功进行和平请愿，而被北京警方抓捕，并被关押于北京市团河劳教所，直至一年多后方予以释放。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日因其屡次控告迫害法轮功的元凶江泽民，遂被当地警方从家中抓走，并被以涉邪教罪刑拘，其家遭查抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被双城区检察院转正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被哈尔滨双城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，后虽经哈尔滨市中级法院二审，但依然维持原判。目前在黑龙江省呼兰监狱服刑。据悉，因在狱中遭遇虐待，致其长期不能排尿而被强制打针。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵海通：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1961</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日出生，青海省海西州人，新疆民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。因长期致力于为新疆地区弱势群体、维吾尔族群体及政治犯、良心犯等维权呼吁，近年来又南下广东，积极与南方各地维权公民、人权捍卫者等一起参与街头民主运动，举行各种声援举牌和集会活动，故而在所处之地备受民众欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，曾因前往湖北武汉会见人权活动家秦永敏，惨遭武汉警方的野蛮殴打，差点丧命；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因努力表达维权公民正当合法的诉求，而不惧风险在广州火车站多次举牌，宣传民主理念，“抗议流氓政府打压民主人士”等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因参与声援安徽民主人士张林之女张安妮失学事件，而遭警方强行拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，曾因在新疆吐鲁番市帮助维吾尔族公民进行维权，而被新疆警方刑拘，并被关押于新疆乌鲁木齐市六道湾看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被新疆警方宣布以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，终被新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市法院以同罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区塔城市乌苏市乌苏监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵怀国：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省张家界市慈利县伯特利家庭教会牧师。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被涉“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US"> 4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被批捕。赵怀国牧师于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年从东北来到湖南，为湖南张家罪培养了一批同工，同时也在慈利县建立了伯特利教会，并在教会服待达<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年之久。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员，哈尔滨市轴承厂退休职工，现年已经七十岁了。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午，赵林在南岗区先锋路附近粘贴了一张“法轮大法好”不干胶，被南岗公安分局国保警察抓捕、抄家，抢走其家中法轮大法书籍。后获悉被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵明堂：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省侯马市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月中旬赵明堂于被判刑四年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵明堂是<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右在侯马市新田广场发真相资料时被警察绑架的，当天晚上被警察赵建林带人非法抄了家。第十天时，赵明堂被非法批捕。十一月中旬在曲沃法院被非法开庭时，赵明堂的儿子与弟弟进入了法庭。开庭中，赵明堂被戴手铐、脚镣，他大声喊“法轮大法好”。赵明堂曾在山西祁县监狱被非法关押七年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵淑玉：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，山东省烟台市莱山区公安分局跨区出动大量警力，将一群手无寸铁的老太太绑架。这群人中<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁以上的就有四位（<span lang="EN-US">79</span>岁的吴香仃，<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁的张慧英，<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁的韩忠香，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁的肖淑娴）；<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁以上的也有四位（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁的邹本珍，<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁的李爱茹，<span lang="EN-US">63</span>岁的马玉珍，<span lang="EN-US">63</span>岁的孙明秋），除此之外，还有赵淑玉，潘荣卿，潘艳岩，栾景尧（潘艳岩的丈夫），崔德英（另案处理）等人。目前，潘荣卿、潘艳岩、马玉珍、赵淑玉被关押于条件恶劣的烟台市福山看守所；韩忠香、肖淑娴、吴香仃、孙明秋、邹本珍被取保候审于原籍；张慧英现被监视居住于家中。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，莱山区检察院罔顾法律、事实，将上面十名无辜法轮功学员构陷到烟台市莱山区法院。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵天慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北高阳县访民。因为在福建省做批发毛巾生意时发生火灾烧了她的库房和门市，赵天慧不满造成事故方的赔偿数额开始上访。随后高阳县政府赶到福建协助处理着火事故，但高阳县政府却在赵天慧不同意赔偿数额的情况下私自做主结案，并拿回了数十万元的赔偿款。赵天慧为此上访已经<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，期间被多次拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，赵天慧进京上访被高阳县公安局行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被转为刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵婷婷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省绥化市北林区法轮功学员。幼师，是九零后，在绥化博洋幼儿园工作。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，绥化市法轮功学员杨传厚、白霞、王芳、王福华、赵婷婷去兰西县北安村发送法轮功资料，被兰西县公安国保和北安镇派出所警察抓捕，关押在兰西县拘留所。后<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被黑龙江省安达市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵文静</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵文静、黄金桔、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵熙茹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵兴有：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江法轮功学员赵兴有，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">79</span>岁，和老伴史桂芝，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十七岁，家住黑龙江省哈尔滨市双城区水泉乡。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，双城房产一工作人员去赵兴有夫妇所居住的水泉乡赵家村一村民家，给该村民的房屋拍照，发现赵兴有夫妇家的院墙上喷写有“法轮大法好”的字样，此工作人员心生恶念，把字样拍照下来，传给双城区公安局、六一零。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，警察将赵兴有夫妇抓捕。送哈尔滨做身体检查后，因史桂芝身体不合格，被放回家，赵兴有被劫持到双城看守所，关押六天放回。放回后，指使保人监视他们，不准往墙上写字、不准去炼功点、不准接触修炼人等。后双城公安局警察将赵兴有、史桂芝夫妇构陷到哈尔滨市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，法院法逮捕通知书，水泉乡派出所苏永生等又将赵兴有、史桂芝夫妇再次绑架，赵兴有被劫持到双城看守所非法关押，史桂芝因检查身体不合格放回。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，史桂芝再次被非法抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月上旬，赵兴有被冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，史桂芝被冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。史桂芝被劫持到黑龙江省女子监狱，赵兴有被劫入哈尔滨市呼兰监狱。赵兴有刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郑明辉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省汕头市法轮功学员。因信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被汕头市公安局金平分局警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被汕头市中级法院终审裁定判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。</b><span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被关押在广东省四会监狱迫害至现在。监狱方为强迫郑明辉思想转化，每天强迫他坐小凳子十几个小时身体不能动、不能睡，用这种阴损的手段长时间折磨他，睡眠严重不足，致使他身心受到很大伤害。郑明辉为抵制监狱对他的强制洗脑转化的迫害，开始绝食。绝食期间，在监狱主管警察操控下，郑明辉头部被犯人狠打五十多下，身体多处被打伤。到<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，已绝食将近五十天。整个人消瘦只剩下七十来斤，变成皮包骨了，精神状态极端不好。他的右额头靠近眉毛处有一块已经结痂的伤疤，头部头发下面有大块的乌青瘀血，手臂也有几处乌青的伤痕。妻子彭佩珊为制止四会监狱继续迫害已生命垂危的丈夫，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月份彭佩珊把四会监狱迫害、打伤郑明辉相关责任人，依法向广东省肇庆市检察院提起控告，并逐级向有关部门抄送报告。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郑书梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">济南法轮功学员、女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十岁。郑书梅、程淑香是在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日分别被槐荫区公安警察有预谋抓捕的，被非法抄家，至今被关押在济南看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日济南市槐荫区法院宣判：郑书梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，程淑香被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。郑书梅刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郑喜林</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">43</span>岁，黑龙江省齐齐哈尔市龙江县人，原齐齐哈尔市昂昂溪区机务段的职工，法轮功学员。因信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年被当局绑架、毒打，后被冤判徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日因被龙江县国保怀疑挂法轮功真相条幅，而被再次绑架。关押期间，遭到国保警察的刑讯逼供，企图逼他提供所谓的“线索”，脸被打破，鲜血直流。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被齐齐哈尔市龙江县法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。其不服，已提出上诉，并绝食抗议非法判刑，绝食一个多月，生命危急。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郑旭飞</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：男，<span lang="EN-US">42</span>岁，山东省乳山市下初镇中心学校体育教师，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，郑旭飞曾因宣传法轮功信息而被警方抓捕，在抓捕过程中，因野蛮抓捕，当被警察拖上警车时，他的锁骨已被摔成骨折，之后被送往看守所刑拘。被关押期间，被戴着手铐脚镣<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月，并遭毒打和被逼做奴工。<span lang="EN-US">35</span>天后被强迫交<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元钱准予取保候审。因他被无理关押迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年的绩效工资两万元被他所在单位扣除。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，郑旭飞又因宣传法轮功资料而被乳山市警方抓捕，后被乳山市检察院正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被乳山市法院以<span lang="EN-US">“</span>利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪<span lang="EN-US">”</span>冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，山东省威海中级法院二审维持非法，并追加罚款罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钟武</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：重庆市人，民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被重庆市警方抓走，被控寻衅滋事的原因是他们所谓“威胁”、“恐吓”重庆渝北法院长周铁等人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，因言获罪，其被重庆市渝北区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被渝北区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转正式批捕，控其因在推特上发推等，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其案被重庆市涪陵区检察院提起公诉，移交至涪陵区法院；至今未判。目前被羁押于重庆市涪陵区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 84.0pt;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钟晓霖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">深圳网友。因为涉及“全国旅游群”为良心犯送饭事，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被当地警方刑拘，一个月后转为指定监视居住，家属低调配合也没有逃脱厄运，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月已经被控煽动颠覆国家政权罪正式逮捕。刑拘期间，人权律师会见了两次。以后改指定监视居住六个月。之后再变更为煽动颠覆罪逮捕，又羁押在深圳宝安看守所。律师曾去要求会见，但不给会见。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 84.0pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钟兴秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西省武宁县人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年期间，曾因组织、参与制作、印刷法轮功宣传光盘、书刊等行动，传授打印、刻录、装订技术等，而遭到地方当局严密监控和打击。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在与他人搬运、携带<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年神韵晚会光盘、《明慧周刊》等相关海外法轮功影像杂志资料时，被武宁县警方获悉，当场拘捕，其家被抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被江西省武宁县人民法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，经九江市中级人民法院二审依然驳回起诉，维持原判。目前被羁押于江西省武宁县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钟怡君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁，吉林省长春市人，上海市贝尔公司退休职工，上海市普陀区新村路真金路万里小区居民，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因笃信法轮功，早年曾于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被警方秘密抓捕，之后长期失联，直至半年之后家人才得知她已被逮捕，后被上海市普陀区法院以邪教罪冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，但判刑后仍长期下落不明。出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初，因其发放法轮功真相资料而再被警方抓捕，失联<span lang="EN-US">1</span>各月后，获悉她被刑拘于上海市普陀区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其案在上海市普陀区法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其被宣判以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。其不服提出上诉，但法院称对其仍然维持原判。目前被关押在上海市普陀区看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">仲周（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年出生，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州人，又叫“尊珠”，阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因其协助侄子兼徒弟、同寺僧人彭措（又叫平措，已于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日自焚死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁）为纪念中共当局镇压拉萨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>•<span lang="EN-US">14</span>事件三周年，抗议中共政府对藏人的强权高压统治，以自焚方式（指一种藏人抗议暴政、伸张正义的方式，即藏人自焚者把自己整个奉献出来，以清晰的理智、自愿的心态和惨烈的方式向暴政表达最强烈抗议的无奈选择，以期使公众舆论对极权和高压统治者予以最强烈的谴责或改变对手的情感）在阿坝县城洽唐中街实施自焚行动；同时，因其担心当局野蛮抢夺自焚尸体，而将自焚后的彭措转移隐藏到格尔登寺内，由此引发中共军警与当地僧人、藏人的激烈对抗和冲突；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其随被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康县警方抓捕，并被以“安排转移、藏匿彭措达<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个小时之久，导致彭措因为体表大面积烧伤、延误救治而死亡”为罪由刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被四川省马尔康县法院以“故意杀人罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周翠萍<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省连云港市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，连云港市海州区公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘玉萍、邵世玲、那仁志、熊成霞、周翠萍、马宝玲、高建君、王艾芝、汪宝玉、小周女士、乔老太等十一人。所有人家中都被非法抄了家，警察劫走家中的电脑、手机、光盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、电器、钱财、书籍等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，周翠萍被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周发明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川绵阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午，周发明在公园散步，被穿着便衣的警察绑架。警察在不通知家人的情况下将其绑架到看守所关押，家人于两天后才知道此事，随后找到派出所。家人找到派出所，起诉派出所的人程序违法。他们随后才补交了一份通知书，由一个开包子店的人转交，让家人自己去取。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日对周发明进行判刑三年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周海燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。周海燕刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周金莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省郴州市永兴县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十一岁的周金莲是永兴县的一个普通家庭妇女，家住湖南省郴州市永兴县沙子光。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，周金莲在永兴县鲤鱼塘镇向民众讲述法轮功真相，被鲤鱼塘派出所的警察抓捕，之后被关押在郴州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬，周金莲被永兴县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周金霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁大连基督徒。曾数十次给习近平、彭丽媛传福音，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被控寻衅滋事遭大连市公安局西岗分局刑事拘留。被控罪名是寻衅滋事。目前羁押在大连市看守所。两年前，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日她曾在在中南海门前举起写着：“神爱世人，呼召习近平、彭丽媛。‘自由、平等、公正、诚信是来自神的，‘无神论’生产罪恶、祸国殃民。公义使邦国高举，罪恶是人民的羞辱！天国近了，你们应当悔改！”随后周金霞被警察扣押、没收了福音信。后被指控是非法上访，扰乱了社会秩序，被大连市公安局于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10 </span>天。而<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，周金霞也曾因在中南海门前传福音被行政拘留过<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。而这一次对周金霞却是刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周糢珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川古蔺县古蔺镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，法轮功学员周糢珍和骆雪梅在习水县醒民镇钢铁村，告诉百姓法轮功真相，被举报。醒民镇派出所抓捕了周糢珍和骆雪梅<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，周糢珍和骆雪梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周启良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周启良、王传煌、汪黎明三人均系江西省武宁县人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年期间，曾因组织、参与制作、印刷法轮功宣传光盘、书刊等行动，学习、传授打印、刻录、装订等技术，使用具有自动拨号及语音功能的手机给他人打电话等，而遭到地方当局严密监控和打击。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在共同搬运、携带<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年神韵晚会光盘、《明慧周刊》等相关海外法轮功影像杂志资料时，被武宁县警方获悉，当场拘捕，其家分别被抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人均被江西省武宁县人民法院一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。其三人均表不服，提起上诉，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，经九江市中级人民法院二审依然驳回起诉，维持原判。目前都被羁押于江西省武宁县看守所。分别刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周世峰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，河南省安阳县人，北京锋锐律师事务所主任，<span lang="EN-US"> 2009</span>年度、<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年度“社会公益法律服务先进个人”、<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年中国法律援助“优秀援助律师”、<span lang="EN-US"> 2009-2011</span>年度“北京优秀律师”，知名人权律师。自<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年执业以来，曾代理过多起著名的受害人案件，并于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月创立北京锋锐律师事务所，广纳包括王宇、刘晓原、王全章等在内的著名人权律师。<span lang="EN-US"> 2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被北京市警方以“严重扰乱社会秩序”、“教唆、组织、策划、资助他人炒作所谓敏感案件” 等为罪由抓走刑拘，其锋锐律师事务所及其办公室被查抄。被指定居所监视居住，其锋锐律师事务所及其办公室被查抄；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被天津市警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被天津市第二中级法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。现羁押在天津市第一看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周维林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽合肥人权捍卫者、工伤致残人士。周维林于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被合肥市公安局瑶海分局城东派出所（电话：<span lang="EN-US">0551-64483496</span>）秘密抓走了。周维林<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，原安徽省拖拉机厂退休职工，维权网信息员，安徽省维权人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年曹顺利人权捍卫者奖获得者。曾于<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日因工受伤，成为丧失劳动能力的伤残人员，但原所在单位一直不给于办理伤残认定和退休等手续，自此走上维权之路。自<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年起，尤其是<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年期间，因长期坚持实名报导安徽及全国各地多种公权力违法侵权事件，并成为“维权网”信息员，而招致当局的强烈不满和忌恨，曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次被合肥警方处以行政拘留，并且多次被警方抄家、传唤、威胁甚至殴打。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，各地维权人士发起声援“安妮失学事件”的活动，周维林因前往进行实时报导，而被合肥警方于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日强行带走，处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又因参与合肥网友聚餐纪念<span lang="EN-US">64</span>活动，遭到警方的报复性拘留，之后获释；但时至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，合肥警方再次因<span lang="EN-US">64</span>纪念活动而以“涉嫌虚构事实扰乱公共秩序”事由对其进行传唤，并处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，合肥警方第三次以参与声援安妮失学事件，维护安妮受教育权活动为由，将其与张林、李化平、姚诚等维权人士一同拘捕，并以涉嫌“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”而刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被当地检察院以同罪名正式批捕，之后被安徽省合肥市地方法院以“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，刑满获释。出狱后仍然在一直坚持为劳工和残疾人维权。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周向阳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津法轮功学员。周向阳从北方交通大学毕业后，分配到天津铁道第三勘探设计院工经处，因工作出色，单位送他到天津大学，又获得投资经济学位；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>考取了全国首批造价工程师职业资格，成为当时全国仅有的六十位造价工程师之一。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，期间遭受无数酷刑：被彻夜电击至遍体鳞伤、连续三十天熬夜、多次关小号、野蛮灌食等等。周向阳在<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被绑架后，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，后到天津市滨海监狱原五监区二分监区（现六监区）服刑，一直绝食抵制迫害。一开始，狱警安排六个包夹人（监狱安排的专门负责看管法轮功学员的刑事罪犯人）白天晚上轮流看管周向阳，每天包夹人用担架抬着周向阳去监狱的医院灌食三次。据包夹人说：“有一次给周向阳灌食，包夹人按着他的胳膊和双腿，监狱医院的人强行把胃管从周向阳的嘴里插进去，灌完食之后，周向阳自己把胃管拔出来，管子上面沾满了鲜血。”妻子李珊珊因坚持为丈夫申冤，曾遭到监狱的报复，两次被非法劳教共计三年多。二零一三年劳教制度解体了，李珊珊是从石家庄女子劳教所走出来的最后一个。一家人团聚的日子没有多久。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日早晨七点，天津警察再一次破门而入，把周向阳和妻子李珊珊抓走了。周向阳被冤判七年，李珊珊被冤判六年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周新宝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省轻工机械厂退休职工，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁，住武汉市武昌区徐家棚街二桥社区，因他家房子被强拆而上访。在上访的过程中，周新宝开始帮助武汉各地的拆迁户和访民们，为他们维权出谋划策，成为当天一名活跃的维权人士。因七一中共党庆期间的<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，武汉一、二百访民集体到北京上访，周新宝被认为是组织者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，周新宝被武昌区杨园派出所警察叫走后刑拘，后家属得知其被关押于武汉安康医院。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>号家属获悉周新宝被逮捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周兴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大连市金州区石河镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，谷秀华（女）、刘希永（男）、周兴（男）、李天学（男）、王丽志（女）、张三曼（女）、谭春荣（女）、孙宝英（女）、刘井龙（男），去大连市金普新区炮台镇袁屯村发放新书《共产主义的终极目的》，被炮台镇派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午二在大连市金州法院庭审。后谷秀华、周兴、王丽志，被大连市金州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；张三曼、谭春荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，李天学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘希永、孙宝英、刘井龙的情况还不清楚。周兴刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周亚平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省成都市双流区人，法轮功信仰者、良心犯。因信仰、宣传法轮功，而被成都市龙泉驿区警方以涉嫌邪教罪抓捕、刑拘，后被转正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日其案被成都市龙泉驿区法院以邪教罪秘密诬判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，其不服，当庭提出上诉。据悉，因要做无罪辩护，法院在审判前未通知其辩护律师到场。目前被羁押在成都市龙泉驿区看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周研：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">46</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。周研被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周彝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省南京市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">81</span>岁，海军航空工程学院退休副教授，大校军衔，师级离休干部。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，周彝与顾素梅（<span lang="EN-US">78</span>岁）在杜惠英（<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁）家学法时，被闯入的鼓楼区公安分局、国保大队及华侨路派出所警察共二、三十人绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月初，周彝的诉江状在明慧网登出后（《海军大校周彝控告迫害元凶江泽民》），就一直处于警察的监控、跟踪之中，并遭强制采血。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，周彝老人遭江苏南京鼓楼区法院庭审，后被判刑，刑期待查。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周友良：<span lang="EN-US">2</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，江苏省无锡、宜兴两市<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余维权人士来到宜兴市拘留所迎接两会期间被行政拘留的维权人沈方明出狱，不料他已被其辖区派出所提前接走，随后大家前往沈方明的家中为他接风洗尘。事后，当大家前往火车站查看返程车次时，却遭到大批特警的抓捕。目前已知，其中任美娇、钱采芹、夏建妹、周友良、汤永斌、王培成<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人被刑拘。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周远志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周远志（笔名华梁兴、曾仁全）<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日生。是一名自由撰稿人、独立中文笔会会员，由于长期撰写、发表关于各类社会问题及揭露官员腐败的文章，在<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被湖北省钟祥市国家安全局以“涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪”抓捕，获释后周远志在家长期被当局监视居住。根据独立中文笔会的网页显示，他以笔名曾仁全发表多篇敏感文章，其中题目包括“农民以特殊方式表达对江泽民的憎恶”及“人民的名义远离普世价值”。周远志被<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被以“织非法聚集罪”刑事拘留。此前，周远志被指组织访民上访而被当局关押，，被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天原本应于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日释放，但未获释放，随后，被确认其在<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日即遭湖北荆门市公安局东宝分局以“织非法聚集罪”刑事拘留。其妻子张中凤说由于他一向身体不好，她非常担心丈夫的情况。现羁押在荆门市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日在荆门掇刀法院开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日以“组织非法聚集罪判刑期<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，网上寻衅滋事罪<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，诽谤罪<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，决定合并执行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月”，刑期<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。目前关押地址：湖北省荆门市东宝区牌楼镇荆门看守所，电话<span lang="EN-US">0724-8882273</span>，邮编<span lang="EN-US">448121<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周育琴</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：广东省惠东县人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信仰、宣传法轮功，周育琴与石雪梅、刘庆强三人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被惠东县政法委、<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办及国保等警方非法抓捕，后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被广东省惠州市惠东县法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密宣判。其中，周育琴被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金五万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）；石雪梅被冤判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）；刘庆强被冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）。三人均不服审判，已向广东省惠州市中级法院提出上诉。目前被关押在惠东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周再强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南长沙网民。职业货车司机。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月网上发言支持香港反送中的光复香港、时代革命运动被刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，周再强的亲友才在微信发出消息称：长沙公民周再强近期因在推特上发言支持香港反送中运动而被当局突然抓捕，并以寻衅滋事的罪名刑事拘留，目前已经确认被关押于长沙市第一看守所。据了解，周再强有两个匿名推特号，已持续发推三万多条。香港反送中运动爆发后，他一直都非常关注，也自发和转发了很多推文表示关注和支持。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱承志：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日因祭奠林昭后已遭强迫失踪，后获知其被控“寻衅滋事”而被指定居所监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林昭祭日当天，朱承志另外<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名维权人士，成功到达苏州灵岩山林昭墓前祭奠。随后，大批警察当场把<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人带走，当中<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人后来获释，但朱承志却和外界失去联系。朱承志早年与友人合资在云南经营锰矿场，其后被新加入的拍档施计夺去矿场，而对方更抢先入禀法院状告朱承志侵吞矿场。结果，朱承志被判败诉，多年资产化为乌有。他多次向公安厅投诉均不获受理，只好进京上访，却遭关押<span lang="EN-US">40</span>天。朱承志遂在网上组织民间维权运动，包括声援“福州三网友”案。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，他又冒险到医院探望近乎失聪失明的同乡兼同窗“六四铁汉”李旺阳，并协助香港媒体为李作生前唯一一次专访。由于他拒绝在“不再关注李旺阳死亡事件保证书”上签字，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被湖南省公安厅以“扰乱社会治安”之名拘留；其家人于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日收到朱承志的逮捕通知书，指朱承志被省公安控以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。后获释。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月与谭作人、艾晓明共同荣获中国民主教育基金会颁发的<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年度杰出民主人士奖。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱凤英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱桂贞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东泰安市法轮功信徒，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁的老太太，原泰安市木器厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日下午，朱桂贞和平秀英为了让民众了解法轮大法，在邱家店镇某村，发送法轮功资料，并向路人讲述法轮功受迫害的真相，遭邱家店派出所警察绑架，被关到泰安市看守所。后于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，朱桂贞因修炼法轮功，向百姓传播法轮大法，被泰安市泰山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱恒德：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省东营市胜利油田年近七十岁法轮功学员，胜利油田孤岛采油厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">19</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日下午，朱恒德正在家看孙子，滨海公安局海滨分局（原胜利油田公安处孤岛公安分处）孤岛国保大队长带人闯入到朱恒德家，抄家两个来小时，强行收缴个人物品，并将朱恒德绑架到东营市牛庄看守所（拘留所）拘留。据称，朱恒德因贴真相资料，被受不明真相的人诬告，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，山东省东营市法院判处朱恒德<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱惠来：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生年月不详，广东省湛江市人，广东省湛江市东海岛东山镇调青北园村村民，抗强拆维权者，民间誉名“东海岛英雄”，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年以来，广东省湛江市政府以“湛江钢铁基地”为名，在无任何批文的前提下（注：该批文直至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日才拿到，总值人民币<span lang="EN-US">700</span>亿），烂用公权，派出大批警力对该区域东海岛东简镇衔头村、迈奴村、蓄昌村等八条村以及东山镇北园村等一万多名村民进行暴力拆迁，致使万民怨声载道；因之前朱惠来父子一家不愿意为强拆签字，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，湛江市开发区官员随带领数十人，在没有支付拆迁款的情况下，强毁其田地和家园里的果树、帐棚和农作物等；其子朱培忍开车回来，看到父亲被警方殴打，随前往和其一起与警方、强拆官员发生激烈对抗，最终导致<span lang="EN-US">1</span>死多伤（其中致当地治安大队副队长死亡）；随后，其立即被警方刑拘和逮捕，但却被民间誉为“东海岛英雄”。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被广东省湛江市赤坎区中级法院以“故意杀人罪”、“故意伤害罪”一审判处死刑；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，经湛江市赤坎区中级法院二审，改判死缓；其不服，继续上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，广东省高级法院对其案以“事实不清、证据不足”为由“撤销原判、发还重审”；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东省湛江市中级法院再次重审朱惠来父子抗强拆杀官员案，最终结果暂时缺详。目前被羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱家彩：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵州毕节威宁县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十多岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因发放法轮功资料挂横幅，朱家彩、罗翠琴遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在毕节七星关区法院被庭审，后得知朱家彩被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款二万元、罗翠琴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索罚款一万元。朱家彩刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱培忍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：出生年月不详，广东省湛江市人，广东湛江东海岛东山镇调青北园村村民，“东海岛英雄”，抗暴维权者。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年以来，广东省湛江市政府以“湛江钢铁基地”为名，在无任何批文的前提下（注：该批文直至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日才拿到，总值人民币<span lang="EN-US">700</span>亿），烂用公权，派出大批警力对该区域东海岛东简镇衔头村、迈奴村、蓄昌村等八条村以及东山镇北园村等一万多名村民进行暴力拆迁，致使万民怨声载道；因之前朱培忍和其父一家不愿意为强拆签字，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，湛江市开发区官员随带领数十人，在没有支付拆迁款的情况下，强毁其父田地和家园里的果树、帐棚和农作物等，其父被严重殴打；其开车回来，看到父亲被警方殴打，随上前与父亲一起与警方、强拆官员发生激烈对抗，最终导致<span lang="EN-US">1</span>死多伤，其随被警方拘捕，但被民间誉为“东海岛英雄”。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被广东省湛江市赤坎区中级法院以“故意杀人罪”、“故意伤害罪”一审判处死缓。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月经湛江市赤坎区中级法院二审，改判为无期徒刑。其依然不服，继续上诉，至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，广东省高级法院对其案以“事实不清、证据不足”为由“撤销原判、发还重审”。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日湛江市中级法院再审朱惠来父子抗暴杀官案，最终结果一直不详。目前被关押地点不详。其在看守所惨遭酷刑，肝部被打裂，生殖器被打烂，牙齿被打掉，为此曾被送医院抢救。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱雪梅</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：贵州省贵阳市人，法轮功学员。因信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日竟在回四川老家照顾<span lang="EN-US">89</span>岁老母的旅途中，在贵阳市火车站被贵阳市南明区警方拦截、绑架、搜查和审讯，次日其家被非法查抄，其被转押至二戈寨派出所拘留。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日晚朱雪梅被迫害的身体出现异常，派出所不得不送其到医院进行检查和紧急救治。之后二戈寨社区人员又将其押送到贵阳市花溪区金竹镇烂泥沟，在洗脑班进行数月思想转化。因其拒绝洗脑转化，再次被送到贵阳市南明区看守所关押，但看守所因其身体检查不合格拒收，其最终被送到贵州省武警总队医院戒毒治疗中心予以关押，至今不予释放，而其身体状况令人堪忧。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱薏：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，广东深圳南山、福田公安警察同时出动，非法抓捕了七位法轮功学员，分别是杨波、肖颖（杨波妻子）、豆君、朱薏、刘利军（音）、陈小燕与吴治明。其中：刘利军（音）被深圳福田公安抓捕，被关押<span lang="EN-US">39</span>天内获释。吴治明，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，被罗湖公安分局警察绑架并抄家，在罗湖看守所出现高血压，被关押<span lang="EN-US">39</span>天后回家。深圳福田区八卦岭派出所警察绑架法轮功学员朱薏并非法抄家，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日南山法院庭审，主审法官刘付斌。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:
