minor-fareast;">祝亚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">武汉市黄陂区法轮功学员，祝亚是个残疾人，家住武汉市黄陂区前川街，丈夫早逝，她与女儿相依为命。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，祝亚去买菜，被便衣警察拦截。这次抓捕祝亚是由省城“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”亲自操控、指使的，他们闯进家中抄家。武汉市黄陂区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日庭审，被秘密枉判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">珠扎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">现年<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县求吉玛乡索日玛村人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。因政治诉求，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年曾被当局以不详政治罪名抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被警方以涉嫌“组织阿坝民众举办达赖喇嘛<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁寿辰活动”为罪由，从其僧舍强行带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其已被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 119.25pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">珠玛别克<span lang="EN-US">.</span>穆汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">42</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁，新疆阿勒泰市人，阿勒泰市喀拉希力克乡武装部官员，哈萨克族政治犯。曾因被新疆中共当局指控在聊天工具微信“乱说话”，“泄漏中共党内机密”，而于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被阿勒泰市警方刑拘、逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，获悉近期已被新疆阿勒泰市法院以“泄露国家机密罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。据称，其原本在上海读大学的儿子因父亲被判刑，竟遭株连，被校方勒令退学，现已回到新疆家中。其妻子古丽加丽拉也因受牵连，原本在乡政府卫生院工作，也因此被辞退，他本人在银行的<span lang="EN-US">60</span>万元人民币积蓄遭罚没，家里的<span lang="EN-US">50</span>头牛也被政府没收。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">庄金莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福建漳州维权公民。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，李红花母亲庄金莲（<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁）、女儿陈小玲（<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁）被漳州龙海市公安局刑事拘留。李红花（<span lang="EN-US">55</span>岁）本人则在前三日的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被龙海法院以拒不履行法律文书义务的理由司法拘留十五日。后又被龙海公安刑事拘留。一家三代女性被控的罪名都是寻衅滋事，后均转为逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">被指控的所谓犯罪的事实<span lang="EN-US">:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>起诉书指控李红花、庄金莲因对拆迁补偿不满，在<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月间，多次到北京中南海周边非正常上访。并多次被训诫和处罚。其中李红花被训诫<span lang="EN-US">16</span>次，庄金莲<span lang="EN-US">14</span>次，陈小玲<span lang="EN-US">6</span>次。福建漳州维权公民李红花一家三代女性被控寻衅滋事罪案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日在漳州女子看守所内开庭审理，未宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">庄友布：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">42</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁，福建省宁德市福鼎县人，法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，与肖传雄、金丽燕、陈星光、杨贵媚、杨雄、陈开奇，林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄，至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，庄友布被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，庄友布被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">追魂（刘进兴）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本名刘进兴，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年出生于湖北大冶，毕业于湖北省美术学院，艺术家，现居北京通州宋庄，从事艺术创作。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，因策划“敏感地带”行为艺术展，被刑事拘留一个月，罪名为“寻衅滋事”。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，因与其他艺术家一道举牌抗议劳教制度，被刑事拘留一个月，罪名为“聚众扰乱社会秩序”。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，因声援争取“真普选”的香港市民，遭到逮捕，被羁押九个月零两天，罪名为“寻衅滋事”，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，以“不予起诉”为名获无罪释放。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午，艺术家追魂与宋庄五位艺术家原国镭、贾穹、庞勇、赵金鹤、程延安在良心运动在中国巡展途中南京被失联。六位艺术家的电话、微信全联系不上。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，南京市公安局玄武分局对追魂北京的家进行了搜查，带走了追魂的早期创作、书籍、艺术作品等，并对追魂的妻子做了询问笔录。在刘立娇（追魂妻子）追问下，告知：追魂涉嫌寻衅滋事罪，已经被刑事拘留，没有给家属相关法律文书。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卓嘎（藏）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省甘孜藏族自治州石渠县色须镇人。藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。卓嘎在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被强行传唤和羁押；后其很快被地方检察院以不明罪由转正式逮捕，并关押于石渠县公安局内；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被以旺青同案犯，以“与他人相勾结、泄露危害国家与地方安全的机密”罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">子肃：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日出生，成都人，<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年毕业于云南大学政治系，到云南省委党校任教，期间有二年挂职任副县长，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年退休。子肃是中共党内公开支持民主宪政的党员之一，主张立即进行彻底的政治民主化改革。退休后积极参与民间维权运动，同时在网络上以其大胆言论而着称。子肃<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年底回到故乡成都。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，子肃在成都东门大桥府河边被成都国家安全局带走。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被成都国家安全局以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，羁押于四川省成都第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，子肃取保获释回到家中。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日子肃以中共党员的身份了发表公开信——《关于在中共十九大上开放党内民主直选和选举胡德平先生为新一届中共总书记的建议》后，再次被带走，现在被收监。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月子肃</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">被以“颠覆国家政权罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">字会梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">鞠殿红、梁琴、张红艳、字会梅、杨顺祥、张绍彩六人皆为基督徒，云南省临沧市云县基督教传道人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年因在云南省多地<span lang="EN-US">/</span>州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>市传道和发展信徒，随被当局以涉嫌“参与三班仆人派邪教组织”为罪由抓捕，其住处所在地遭查抄，搜走传道宣传品<span lang="EN-US">1831</span>份、传单<span lang="EN-US">2556</span>份，并从电子设备中提取到的电子文件<span lang="EN-US">82816</span>个等。后被云南省临沧市云县检察院宣布正式批捕，并被指控<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人是邪教骨干分子，“到云南省多地州市秘密聚会、传经布道和发展信徒，继续鼓吹、宣扬世界末日论，培养组织骨干，为秘密传教布道聚会创造条件和提供便利，重建‘三班仆人派’组织体系等”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人分别被云南省临沧市云县法院以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月到<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等。其中，鞠殿红因是要犯，被重判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年；梁琴因是要犯被重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。杨顺祥判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">其余张红艳、字会梅、张绍彩<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人，具体刑期不详。但此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人都因不服判决，都已提起上诉</b>。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邹昌英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">家住西昌市西郊乡张家屯村三组。邹昌英<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份和小庙乡拆迁户到北京上访，举报村文书张荣康倒卖本组安置自用地举报材料转下来，西昌市公安局外南派出所民警找邹昌英调查过几次。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日邹昌英被西昌市公安局外南派出所带走并刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日邹昌英被西昌市公安局以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”被逮捕，羁押于西昌市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日此案在西昌市法院审理未判决。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">左洪涛</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局在左洪涛、崔秋荣夫妇开的“佳合中介”抓捕了夫妻二人及吴文章、杨晓勇、袁素静及李国爱等五名法轮功学员，抄查中野蛮地抢劫了中介周转资金十余万元现金及电动车一辆和其它办公用品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，山海关区检察院侦监科科长陈铁忠对左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。左洪涛刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">结束语：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本报告是一份月度动态报告，这是第<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">58</span></b>期，肯定仍然会有遗漏和信息滞后的情况。希望大陆各地的人权捍卫者积极补充，请将符合本报告标准而未统计人员情况、以及本报告名单人员的最新情况提供给我们，以便使以后的报告更加翔实和完善。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、薄长城：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省榆树人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信法轮功而屡遭当局打压迫害，多次被绑架、拘留等。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其及多个法轮功信仰者被秦皇岛公安局海港公安分局国保警察非法闯入家中搜查和绑架，送秦皇岛看守所关押，后被当地法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，在冀东监狱服刑。出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，薄长城与另一名学员宋兴伟带着一块玉器去上海鉴定时，因为喷上法轮大法好的真相字，就被沧州市开发区分局获悉抓捕，关押在市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被转至上海市宝山区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其二人案在上海市宝山区法院正式开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，薄长城和宋兴伟分别被上海市宝山区法枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并罚金一万。目前在上海提篮桥监狱十监区服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: minor-fareast;">、陈利荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大连瓦房店法轮功学员陈桂荣、陈利荣姐妹俩，在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日与法轮功学员王永生配合发放真相资料时，遭恶意举报被抓捕，被瓦房店法院非法开庭并判刑，姐姐陈桂荣遭诬判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，妹妹陈利荣遭诬判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。陈利荣刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 123.75pt;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、陈仲轩：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">甘肃会宁县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十三岁，毕业于甘肃警察学校，曾任职于会宁县公安局，一级警官。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日陈仲轩再次被抓捕，被白银区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被劫持到兰州市大砂坪监狱。陈仲轩陷冤狱一年后才和家人见面，现在情况不明。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、邓传彬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川宜宾人，是一位独立电影拍摄者及积极参与社会事务的行动者。他曾作为艾晓明的助手拍摄乌坎事件，在乡村红丝带行动中帮扶河南艾滋病病人，并参与了众多公民围观事件，如围观王荔蕻开庭案、山东陈光诚案等。自从<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年符海陆、罗富誉、张隽勇及陈兵等以“铭记八酒六四”白酒纪念六四被捕后，酒便和六四纪念扯上关系。酒案四人在不审不判的状态下被羁押近三年，终在今年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月开庭，陈兵判刑三年半，其他三人被处以缓刑。陈兵至今仍在囚。邓传彬（网名晃晃）是<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日于推特上传了一张六四酒案酒瓶照片，被国保带走拘留，涉嫌所谓寻衅滋事。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓传彬（网名晃晃）于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被以寻衅滋事罪为由判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年 已获释回家<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、高一川：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西省榆林市“三赎基督”信徒，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被执行逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被宁夏石嘴山市中级法院二审维持一审，以组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">6</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、姜家文：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁丹东维权人士。姜家文在<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">12</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">12</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">12</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">12</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">12</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被刑拘<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；同年又刑拘<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次合<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个多月：<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被刑拘<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被以“涉嫌颠覆国家政权”刑拘，以“寻滋罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>个月。加上其他<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余次的拘留拘禁，合计姜家文因维权被失去人身自由至少<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多个月。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，姜家文先生被从北京强制遣返回辽宁丹东，在丹东市公安局七道派出所关了七日后以“涉嫌颠覆国政权罪”逮捕，送丹东市看守所羁押。六个月后以“寻衅滋事罪”起诉，罪名是接受新唐人记者采访，在推特发表香港占中意见并拍照上网，声援何斌、徐彩虹、朱小平、李延香等访友，及网罗一些以前被处罚过陈年旧账等等，共计判刑一年六个月。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出狱的全国被“劳教冠军”姜家文，在辽宁省丹东市稳控<span lang="EN-US">70</span>天后返京申诉，原以为推迟的全国“两会”已经结束，可以安心地在帝都伸冤，不料北京闹继发性瘟疫，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月又遭强迫失踪。后获释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李克珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">糜崇标夫人，与糜崇标同时被抓。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，李克珍在长时间的折磨里突发脑梗，地方政府怕承担死人的责任，此时便再次叫糜崇标儿子来到医院，不由分说就必须签下自己母亲的病危通知书。经过紧急抢救，才住院一个星期，病情稍微稳定，就被公安强行带离医院，带到他们拘禁的地方继续暗无天日关押。至今已关押四年多。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，糜崇标儿子糜祖恒和四位律师再次来到贵阳市乌当区检察院查询得知，糜崇标涉嫌故意伤害案该院已于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日（该院<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日受理案件）作出不起诉决定，李克珍不涉案，不起诉决定书不能给亲属，也不能给律师，更离谱的是，虽然检察院已作出不起诉决定，糜崇标和李克珍却没有被释放，依然不知所踪！</span><span style="font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">​​​</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">与糜崇标</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;;">一直被囚禁</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;;">年初才获自由。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、林兰英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福州“<span lang="EN-US">9.12</span>”事件当事人之一。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，福州公民与严兴声太太及亲属共<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多人去迎接严兴声先生出狱，因在福州第一看守所门口放鞭炮，被晋安警方带走。后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，福州市仓山区法院就<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日福州维权人士放鞭炮迎良心犯的福州“鞭炮案”，一审宣判。福州著名维权人士林应强和唐兆星均被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，林兰英判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。林兰英刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘爱英</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市赛罕区人，原呼和浩特市玉泉区化纤厂宿舍简易楼居民，基督徒，呼和浩特市基督教“呼喊派”召会骨干成员，中国在押良心犯。因信仰有争议的基督教地方召会“呼喊派”，拥有“呼喊派”书籍，并与基督徒胡功等人积极散发<span lang="EN-US">800</span>百余份福音宣传资料，触动了中共当局加强意识形态、信仰自由控制的敏感神经，随于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被呼和浩特市玉泉区警方从居住地带走，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”刑事拘留，被羁押于内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，又被以同罪名正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其涉嫌“邪教案”被内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市玉泉区检察院提起公诉，被控以“小排聚会、主日聚会、婚礼聚会、境外特会进行聚集，通过电子邮件接收境外的邪教资料，与境外的邪教人员进行非法联系”；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，最终被呼和浩特市玉泉区法院以“组织和利用邪教破坏国家法律实施”罪重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，经呼和浩特市中级法院二审宣布：驳回上诉，维持原判。目前具体服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、刘淑英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南京法轮功学员。年过八旬。刘淑英在科研部门工作，她丈夫为南京解放军通讯工程学院德高望重的老教授，技术骨干。刘淑英和丈夫孙教授，被南京秦淮区公检法、六一零构陷，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被判刑两年。现刘淑英被非法关押在南京女子监狱，她丈夫孙教授被非法关押在苏州监狱。他们的女儿孙学智<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被构陷发法轮功<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘，被月牙湖派出所警察绑架、关进南京市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被批捕，目前情况不明。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">11</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、罗慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">成都法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，罗慧与张弘在青羊区草堂派出所管辖地马路边贴不干胶，被打扫卫生的环卫工人看见并诬告。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，草堂派出所警察通过天网跟踪到罗慧、张弘家，绑架了她们，并抄家，。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日罗慧、张弘被正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日罗慧、张弘被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，各罚款八千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、马胜才：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省沂水县龙家圈镇柴山村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年六十三岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日下午，马胜才和妻子蔡红花在家中被警方抓捕。此时其妻蔡红花正在院子中洗澡。马胜才被刑事拘留，一个月后的<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被批捕，蔡红花被非法行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。时隔将近一年，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日开庭。马胜才、蔡红花夫妇被秘密判决。马胜才被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年并送入济南监狱，蔡红花被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">不服上诉，临沂市中级法院驳回上诉维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">13</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">糜崇标：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">75</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁，抗日将军之子，贵州人权捍卫者，贵州“人权橱窗”创办者。自小父亲死于政治迫害，糜崇标也从小被送往孤儿院并被奴役造成终身残疾。从<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年开始，糜崇标在贵阳市创办“人权厨窗”、宣传《世界人权宣言》，之后遭遇被谈话，被旅游，被劝离，被监禁…糜崇标成为了地方政府重点“维稳”的对象，手段不断升级。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，糜崇标组织了近千人群众<span lang="EN-US">,</span>在贵阳人民广场拉起横幅《“八九六四”二十三周年祭》，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，贵阳当局派出了一百多位国保、公安和特警，直接冲进糜崇标家里，在不出示任何法律依据、手续的情况下暴力抄家，糜崇标的妻子也被殴打并带走，软禁至今，不给家属出任何监禁、关押糜崇标的手续和相关法律依据。夫妻二人在被关押期间，遭到随意性地殴打与折磨。至今已关押五年多。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，糜崇标夫妇遭到长期非法关押黑监狱里的监控国保代应勇殴打，在被迫自卫时，把监管人员云岩区国保代应勇砍伤，现被关押到贵阳市云岩区白花山看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，糜崇标儿子糜祖恒和四位律师再次来到贵阳市乌当区检察院查询得知，糜崇标涉嫌故意伤害案该院已于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日（该院<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日受理案件）作出不起诉决定，李克珍不涉案，不起诉决定书不能给亲属，也不能给律师，更离谱的是，虽然检察院已作出不起诉决定，糜崇标和李克珍却没有被释放，依然不知所踪！</span><span style="font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">​​​</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">糜崇标和妻子李克珍</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;;">一直被囚禁</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;;">年初才获自由。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">14</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、石泽惠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省太仓市法轮功学员。苏州市太仓市健雄学院教师，因坚持修炼法轮大法，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，石泽惠在太仓的家突遭非法抄家，家属才知道石泽惠已在南通市如东县遭绑架。后其于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月在江苏如东遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被关押到苏州监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">15</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋兴伟：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">42</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁，河北省沧州市人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因笃信法轮功而屡遭当局绑架、非法关押和被酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年，曾被关押在黄骅看守所，期间遭受酷刑摧残，被恶警用带铁钉的板子抽打，他被迫绝食抗议，最后才被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年又被当局抓捕，后被非法冤判判刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。在河北省石家庄监狱服刑期间，曾受尽折磨。当局为了让他放弃信仰，狱中曾被“熬鹰”（不允许睡觉）、殴打，整日坐在倒着放的四条腿的小板凳上，不能动，如果动就被殴打。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因与其他<span lang="EN-US">25</span>名狱中法轮功信仰者集体绝食抗议迫害，竟被狱警长时间铐在窗户上吊打。<a href="https://www.blogger.com/null" name="_Hlk510136663"><span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年</a><span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，他和另一法轮功信仰者薄长城带着一块玉器去上海鉴定时，因为喷上法轮大法好的真相字，就被沧州市开发区分局获悉抓捕，关押在市看守所，三天后被转至上海市宝山区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其二人案在上海市宝山区法院正式开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，宋兴伟和薄长城分别被上海市宝山区法枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并罚金一万。目前在上海提篮桥监狱十监区服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">16</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、魏玉红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京大兴区团河苑小区五十二岁（<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年）的残疾妇女。因向人讲法轮功真相遭抓捕，遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至自<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">17</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">温卫红：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市赛罕区人，原呼和浩特市玉泉区八里庄村居民，私营小业主，基督徒，呼和浩特市基督教“呼喊派”召会骨干成员，中国在押良心犯。因信仰有争议的基督教地方召会“呼喊派”，拥有“呼喊派”书籍，并与基督徒胡功等人积极散发<span lang="EN-US">800</span>百余份福音宣传资料，触动了中共当局加强意识形态、信仰自由控制的敏感神经，随于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被呼和浩特市玉泉区警方从居住地带走，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”刑事拘留，被羁押于内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市第三看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，又被以同罪名正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其涉嫌“邪教案”被内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市玉泉区检察院提起公诉，被控以“小排聚会、主日聚会、婚礼聚会、境外特会进行聚集，通过电子邮件接收境外的邪教资料，与境外的邪教人员进行非法联系”；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，最终被呼和浩特市玉泉区法院以“组织和利用邪教破坏国家法律实施”罪重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，经呼和浩特市中级法院二审宣布：驳回上诉，维持原判。目前具体服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">18</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、杨前：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，合浦县人，现居住北海市。由于家里的砖场遭到广西合浦县常乐镇政府的强拆，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬，杨前和母亲、弟弟便去合浦县常乐镇政府讨说法，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日杨前和母亲丶弟弟被以寻畔滋事罪抓捕。母亲和弟弟于<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日释放监视居住，杨前至今还关押在合浦县看守所。合浦常乐镇派出所是跨县区派出所，办案时没有经过北海市海城区高德派出所民警协助到现场，办案程序违法。杨在新律师会见得知杨前被同仓犯人鸡奸、欧打折磨，向有关部门反映也无人处理。杨前之所以绝食是抗议办案单位的执法不公，即使绝食抗争也没有能够维护自己的基本权利。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被秘密审判，并且当天就被判处<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">19</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、张弘：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">成都法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，罗慧与张弘在青羊区草堂派出所管辖地马路边贴不干胶，被打扫卫生的环卫工人看见并诬告。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，草堂派出所警察通过天网跟踪到罗慧、张弘家，绑架了她们，并抄家，。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日罗慧、张弘被正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日罗慧、张弘被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，各罚款八千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><br /></div>
</div>
